public interface Amazon.Backup.Model.IBackupPaginatorFactory {
    public abstract virtual IListBackupJobsPaginator ListBackupJobs(ListBackupJobsRequest request);
    public abstract virtual IListBackupJobSummariesPaginator ListBackupJobSummaries(ListBackupJobSummariesRequest request);
    public abstract virtual IListBackupPlansPaginator ListBackupPlans(ListBackupPlansRequest request);
    public abstract virtual IListBackupPlanTemplatesPaginator ListBackupPlanTemplates(ListBackupPlanTemplatesRequest request);
    public abstract virtual IListBackupPlanVersionsPaginator ListBackupPlanVersions(ListBackupPlanVersionsRequest request);
    public abstract virtual IListBackupSelectionsPaginator ListBackupSelections(ListBackupSelectionsRequest request);
    public abstract virtual IListBackupVaultsPaginator ListBackupVaults(ListBackupVaultsRequest request);
    public abstract virtual IListCopyJobsPaginator ListCopyJobs(ListCopyJobsRequest request);
    public abstract virtual IListCopyJobSummariesPaginator ListCopyJobSummaries(ListCopyJobSummariesRequest request);
    public abstract virtual IListFrameworksPaginator ListFrameworks(ListFrameworksRequest request);
    public abstract virtual IListLegalHoldsPaginator ListLegalHolds(ListLegalHoldsRequest request);
    public abstract virtual IListProtectedResourcesPaginator ListProtectedResources(ListProtectedResourcesRequest request);
    public abstract virtual IListProtectedResourcesByBackupVaultPaginator ListProtectedResourcesByBackupVault(ListProtectedResourcesByBackupVaultRequest request);
    public abstract virtual IListRecoveryPointsByBackupVaultPaginator ListRecoveryPointsByBackupVault(ListRecoveryPointsByBackupVaultRequest request);
    public abstract virtual IListRecoveryPointsByLegalHoldPaginator ListRecoveryPointsByLegalHold(ListRecoveryPointsByLegalHoldRequest request);
